 darshaniktaa gahari ho jaati he

 lekin gadhy lekhak ke banisbat unka yaayavar or kavi rup zyada sahaj or saral he

 From - 'namghna in the fog is like a starry, very irritating Yakshini of Yaksini!' Write a formal introduction to the unknowable, then it will be something like this
 janm 7 march, 1911 ko kushinagar main hua
 The full name was Sachchidananda Hiranand Vatsyayan 'agnayya'
 hindi ke prasiddh sahityakar the
 Poet, stylist, storyteller, fine-essayist, editor and teacher
 pita pandit hiranand shastri pracheen lipiyon ke visheshgy the
 His childhood was spent revolving around many places with his father's job
 lakhanu, srinagar, jammu ghoomte hue inkaa parivaar 1919 main nalanda pahunchaa
 In Nalanda, Agyeya's father started teaching him Hindi, writing
 saal 1921 main agyeya kaa parivaar uti pahunchaa
 It is here that the father of the Agnayya got him sacrificed and 'vatsyayan; Gave the surname
 agyeya ne ghar par hi bhashaa, sahitya, itihaas or vigyaan kii praarambhik shiksha aarambh kii
 In 1925, Agyeya passed the matriculation private examination from Punjab, followed by two years at Madras Christian College and three years at Forman College, Lahore
 lahore main hi agyeya ne biessi or angrezi main eme purvarddh puraa kiya
 Meanwhile, Bhagat became a companion of Singh and was arrested in 1930
 chah varsh jail or nazarbandi bhogane ke baad jab aaazaad hue to 1936 main kuch dinon tak agra ke samachar patr 'sainik' ke sampadan mandal main rahe
 He was in the editorial department of 'vishal Bharat' in the year 1937-39
 kuch din ol india radio main rahane ke baad agyeya 1943 main sainya seva main pravisht hue
 Freed from military service in 1946, he engaged purely in literature
 meerut or uske baad elahabaad or ant main dilli ko unhone apana centre banaaya
 Agnayya edited 'pratik'
 pratik ne hi hindi ke aadhunik sahitya kii nai dharna ke lekhakon, kaviyon ko ek nayaa shashakt manch diya or saahitiyik patrakarita kaa nayaa itihaas rachaa
 He was the editor of the agnostic weekly 'dinman' from 1965 to 1968
 pun: 1973 se 'pratik' ko nayaa naam diya or 'nayaa pratik' kah nikaalnaa shuru kiya
 In 1977, he took over the editing of the daily paper Navbharat Times and in August 1979 he retired from Navbharat Times
 agyeya ne 1943 main saat kaviyon ke vaktavy or kavitaaon ko lekar ek lambii bhoomika ke saath 'taar saptak' kaa sampadan kiya
 Which holds a special place in Hindi poetry literature
 agyeya ne aadhunik hindi kavita ko ek nayaa mode diya, jise prayogshil kavita kii sangya di jaati he
 He also edited the second octave, third octave and fourth octave
 agyeya kii charchit rachanaaon main 'bhagndoot', 'chintaa', 'ityalam', 'hari ghaas par kshan bhar', 'baavaraa aheri', 'angan ke paar dwaar', 'purva', 'kitni naavon main kitni baar', 'kyonki main use jaanata hoon', 'sagar mudra', 'pehle main sannata bunata hoon', 'shekhar,ek jeevani', 'nadi ke dweep', or 'apane apane ajanabi' shaamil he
 He was honored with the Indian Award, International 'golden Reath' Award, Sahitya Academy Award and Jnanpith Award
 agyeya ne kabhi kaha tha, unke likhe par ungali nahin uthaai ja sakati
 Similarly, writing on them is also a difficult task
 ken upanishad kahata he 'jo usko jaanata he, uske liye wo agyaat he
 He is known to those who do not know him
 ' agyeya bhi aise hi the
 Books, columns, research are all less to write on them
 jivan kii itani bhinnata or itane vividh rup, vipul lekhan

 aaj to ek hi akhbaari kaal sab par aisa haaavee he ki dhire-dhire patra yaa calendar dekhne kaa abhyaas bhi mit rahaa he

 or jin ko radio kii lat he unka bhi yahi haal haih radio bataa detaa he ki aaj koun din he, koun-si tarikh, bas

 India successfully tested Agni-4, an intercontinental ballistic missile capable of carrying nuclear weapons
